THE COMMISSIONER OF LAND ADMINISTRATION DEPARTMENT CHEPAUK, CHENNAI-600 005.
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
FORM C
[See Rule 7]
FORM OF NOTICE UNDER SUB-SECTION(1) OF SECTION 3 OF THE TAMIL NADU ACQUISITION OF 
LANDS FOR INDUSTRIAL PURPOSES ACT, 1997 
(CLA-SIP/2024/40/07/07/0001)
No.VI(1)/692(e-1)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided 
that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or 
managed by the Managing Director, SIPCOT, The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 8.9300 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit,Tiruvallur may be inspected on any day during office hours.

Total extent to be acquired: 8.9300 (Hectares)
(CLA-SIP/2024/40/07/04/0001)
No.VI(1)/692(e-2)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided 
that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or 
managed by the Managing Director, SIPCOT, The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 10.0400 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar (LA), 
Unit, Tiruvallur may be inspected on any day during office hours.

10.0400

10.0400

Total extent to be acquired: 10.0400 (Hectares)
(CLA-SIP/2024/40/04/05/0001)
No.VI(1)/692(e-3)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Managing 
Director, SIPCOT, The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of 
Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 11.3567 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit, Tiruvallur which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

(CLA-SIP/2024/40/08/05/0001)
No.VI(1)/692(e-6)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT, Chennai. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil 
Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 10.2750 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit,Tiruvallur may be inspected on any day during office hours.
Tඐඍ Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ

(CLA-SIP/2024/40/01/10/0001)
No.VI(1)/692(e-7)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT, Chennai. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of Section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 10.7500 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit,Tiruvallur may be inspected on any day during office hours.
Tඐඍ Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ
